At lunch (12:30pm?), accidentally hit the "switch watchface" long gesture, then came back and had
the notification for WearNotificationHelper. Of course, it's not here in the log anywhere. Sigh.
It's *also* not present in the phone's logs. Sigh.

The relevant time here seems to be 13:35:05, where we're initially clipping 0 events then 100ms later
on, we're clipping the full set of events.

Resolution for now:

More debugging in the logs to say the size of the messages we're getting (might be useful, hard to say).
We already dump the message lengths on the phone side, so it will be helpful to have them on the watch side
for comparison.
